\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{zone.\+js\+:}} Deep and legacy {\ttfamily dist/} imports like {\ttfamily zone.\+js/bundles/zone-\/testing.js} and {\ttfamily zone.\+js/dist/zone} are no longer allowed. {\ttfamily zone-\/testing-\/bundle} and {\ttfamily zone-\/testing-\/node-\/bundle} are also no longer part of the package.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The proper way to import {\ttfamily zone.\+js} and {\ttfamily zone.\+js/testing} is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ 'zone.js';}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ 'zone.js/testing';}

\end{DoxyCode}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{zone.\+js\+:}} in Task\+Tracking\+Zone\+Spec track a periodic task until it is cancelled
\end{DoxyItemize}

The breaking change is scoped only to the plugin {\ttfamily zone.\+js/plugins/task-\/tracking}. If you used {\ttfamily Task\+Tracking\+Zone\+Spec} and checked the pending macro\+Tasks e.\+g. using `(this.\+ng\+Zone as any).\+\_\+inner .\+\_\+parent.\+\_\+properties.\+Task\+Tracking\+Zone.\+get\+Tasks\+For(\textquotesingle{}macro\+Task'){\ttfamily , then its behavior slightly changed for periodic macrotasks. For example, previously the}set\+Interval{\ttfamily macrotask was no longer tracked after its callback was executed for the first time. Now it\textquotesingle{}s tracked until the task is explicitly cancelled, e.\+g with}clear\+Interval(id)\`{}.\hypertarget{md__d_1_2_g_i_t_2_food_link_2foodlink_8client_2node__modules_2zone_8js_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md22848}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{\href{https://github.com/angular/angular/compare/zone.js-0.11.4...zone.js-0.11.5}{\texttt{ 0.\+11.\+5}} (2022-\/03-\/03)}{\href{https://github.com/angular/angular/compare/zone.js-0.11.4...zone.js-0.11.5}{\texttt{ 0.\+11.\+5}} (2022-\/03-\/03)}}\label{md__d_1_2_g_i_t_2_food_link_2foodlink_8client_2node__modules_2zone_8js_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md22848}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{zone.\+js\+:}} Zone\+JS no longer swallows errors produced by {\ttfamily Object.\+define\+Property} calls.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Prior to this change, Zone\+JS monkey patched {\ttfamily Object.\+define\+Property} and if there is an error (such as the property is not configurable or not writable) the patched logic swallowed it and only console.\+log was produced. This behavior used to hide real errors, so the logic is now updated to trigger original errors (if any). One exception where the patch remains in place is {\ttfamily document.\+register\+Element} (to allow smooth transition for code/polyfills that rely on old behavior in legacy browsers). If your code relies on the old behavior (where errors were not thrown before), you may need to update the logic to handle the errors that are no longer masked by Zone\+JS patch.

\label{_0.11.1}%
\hypertarget{md__d_1_2_g_i_t_2_food_link_2foodlink_8client_2node__modules_2zone_8js_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md22862}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{\href{https://github.com/angular/angular/compare/zone.js-0.11.0...zone.js-0.11.1}{\texttt{ 0.\+11.\+1}} (2020-\/08-\/19)}{\href{https://github.com/angular/angular/compare/zone.js-0.11.0...zone.js-0.11.1}{\texttt{ 0.\+11.\+1}} (2020-\/08-\/19)}}\label{md__d_1_2_g_i_t_2_food_link_2foodlink_8client_2node__modules_2zone_8js_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md22862}
\hypertarget{md__d_1_2_g_i_t_2_food_link_2foodlink_8client_2node__modules_2zone_8js_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md22863}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Bug Fixes}{Bug Fixes}}\label{md__d_1_2_g_i_t_2_food_link_2foodlink_8client_2node__modules_2zone_8js_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md22863}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{zone.\+js\+:}} zone.\+js package.\+json should not include files/directories field (\href{https://github.com/angular/angular/issues/38528}{\texttt{ \#38528}}) (\href{https://github.com/angular/angular/commit/6b662d1}{\texttt{ 6b662d1}}), closes \href{https://github.com/angular/angular/issues/38526}{\texttt{ \#38526}} \href{https://github.com/angular/angular/issues/38516}{\texttt{ \#38516}} \href{https://github.com/angular/angular/issues/38513}{\texttt{ \#38513}}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__d_1_2_g_i_t_2_food_link_2foodlink_8client_2node__modules_2zone_8js_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md22864}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{BREAKING CHANGES since Zone.\+js v0.\+11.\+1}{BREAKING CHANGES since Zone.\+js v0.\+11.\+1}}\label{md__d_1_2_g_i_t_2_food_link_2foodlink_8client_2node__modules_2zone_8js_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md22864}
Prior to {\ttfamily v0.\+11.\+1}, Zone.\+js provided two distribution bundle formats in the {\ttfamily dist} folder. They were (1) {\ttfamily ES5} bundle distributed as {\ttfamily zone.\+js} and (2) {\ttfamily ES2015} bundle distributed as {\ttfamily zone-\/evergreen.\+js}. These bundles are used for Angular\textquotesingle{}s differential-\/loading mechanism.

Prior to {\ttfamily v0.\+11.\+11} the following code


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ 'zone.js';}

\end{DoxyCode}


would load the {\ttfamily ES5} bundle from {\ttfamily dist/zone.\+js}.

Starting with {\ttfamily v0.\+11.\+1}, Zone.\+js follows the \href{https://docs.google.com/document/d/1CZC2rcpxffTDfRDs6p1cfbmKNLA6x5O-NtkJglDaBVs}{\texttt{ Angular Package Format}}, so the folder structure of the Zone.\+js bundles is updated to match {\ttfamily Angular Package Format}. So the same code


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ 'zone.js';}

\end{DoxyCode}


now loads the {\ttfamily ES2015} bundle instead.

This is a breaking change for legacy browsers such as {\ttfamily IE11}.

For backwards compatibility {\ttfamily zone.\+js} continues to distribute the same bundles under {\ttfamily dist}. To restore the old behavior change the {\ttfamily polyfills.\+ts} generated by {\ttfamily Angular CLI} to import like so\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ 'zone.js/dist/zone';}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__d_1_2_g_i_t_2_food_link_2foodlink_8client_2node__modules_2zone_8js_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md23049}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Features}{Features}}\label{md__d_1_2_g_i_t_2_food_link_2foodlink_8client_2node__modules_2zone_8js_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md23049}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{scheduling\+:}} Prefer Mutation\+Observer over Promise in FF (\href{https://github.com/angular/zone.js/commit/038bdd9}{\texttt{ 038bdd9}})
\item {\bfseries{scheduling\+:}} Support Promise.\+then() fallbacks to enqueue a microtask (\href{https://github.com/angular/zone.js/commit/74eff1c}{\texttt{ 74eff1c}})
\item add is\+Root\+Zone api (\href{https://github.com/angular/zone.js/commit/bf925bf}{\texttt{ bf925bf}})
\item make root zone id to be 1 (\href{https://github.com/angular/zone.js/commit/605e213}{\texttt{ 605e213}})
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__d_1_2_g_i_t_2_food_link_2foodlink_8client_2node__modules_2zone_8js_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md23050}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{BREAKING CHANGES}{BREAKING CHANGES}}\label{md__d_1_2_g_i_t_2_food_link_2foodlink_8client_2node__modules_2zone_8js_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md23050}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item New child zones are now created only from a async task that installed a custom zone.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Previously even without a custom zone installed (e.\+g. Long\+Stacktraces\+Zone), we would spawn new child zones for all asynchronous events. This is undesirable and generally not useful.

It does not make sense for us to create new zones for callbacks from the root zone since we care only about callbacks from installed custom zones. This reduces the overhead of zones.

This primarily means that Long\+Stack\+Traces zone won\textquotesingle{}t be able to trace events back to Zone.\+init(), but instead the starting point will be the installation of the Long\+Stacktraces\+Zone. In all practical situations this should be sufficient.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item zone.\+js as well as \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}-\/zone.js files are moved from / to dist/
\end{DoxyItemize}
